16-03-2026 E: 10.16.50#b#E: exe: Get Samsung Mode UUID / Java Code [
     Code: import org.json.JSONArray;
     import org.json.JSONObject;
     import java.util.ArrayList;
     import java.util.HashMap;
     import java.util.List;
     import java.util.Map;
     
     /* Get the input variables from Tasker. */
     String uuidsJsonString = tasker.getVariable("uuids");
     String allRoutinesJsonString = tasker.getVariable("all_routines");
     
     /* Initialize lists to hold parsed data. */
     List targetUuids = new ArrayList();
     List allRoutines = new ArrayList();
     
     /* Parse the uuids JSON array or comma-separated UUID string. */
     if (uuidsJsonString != null && uuidsJsonString.length() > 0) {
         try {
             JSONArray uuidsJsonArray = new JSONArray(uuidsJsonString);
             for (int i = 0; i < uuidsJsonArray.length(); i++) {
                 targetUuids.add(uuidsJsonArray.getString(i));
             }
         } catch (Exception e) {
             tasker.log("UUIDs input is not a JSON array, attempting to split by comma: " + uuidsJsonString);
             String[] parts = uuidsJsonString.split(",");
             for (int i = 0; i < parts.length; i++) {
                 targetUuids.add(parts[i].trim());
             }
         }
     }
     
     /* Parse the all_routines JSON array. */
     if (allRoutinesJsonString != null && allRoutinesJsonString.length() > 0) {
         JSONArray allRoutinesJsonArray = new JSONArray(allRoutinesJsonString);
         for (int i = 0; i < allRoutinesJsonArray.length(); i++) {
             allRoutines.add(allRoutinesJsonArray.getJSONObject(i));
         }
     }
     
     /* Create a new list to store the filtered routine maps. */
     List routineList = new ArrayList();
     
     /* Iterate through all routines and filter them. */
     for (int i = 0; i < allRoutines.size(); i++) {
         JSONObject routine = (JSONObject) allRoutines.get(i);
         String routineUuid = routine.optString("uuid", null);
     
         if (targetUuids.contains(routineUuid)) {
             Map routineMap = new HashMap();
     
             if (routine.has("uuid")) {
                 routineMap.put("uuid", routine.optString("uuid"));
             } else {
                 tasker.log("Field 'uuid' not found in routine object.");
                 routineMap.put("uuid", null);
             }
     
             if (routine.has("name")) {
                 routineMap.put("name", routine.optString("name"));
             } else {
                 tasker.log("Field 'name' not found in routine object.");
                 routineMap.put("name", null);
             }
     
             routineList.add(routineMap);
         }
     }
     
     /* Convert the list of routine maps into a pretty-printed JSON string. */
     String jsonResult = tasker.toJson(routineList, true);
     
     /* Return the generated JSON string to Tasker. */
     return jsonResult;
